Booking Flow: OpenBookingSimpleFlow

Opportunity Type: Multiple

Feature: Core / AgentBroker mode (Implemented)

Test: Customer not included in Order in AgentBroker mode

If customer is not included in Order in AgentBroker mode for C2 or B request, request should fail, returning 400 status code and IncompleteCustomerDetailsError.

Running only this test

npm start -- --runInBand test/features/core/agent-broker/implemented/customer-not-included-test.js

Is this test failing?

  • ‚ö†Ô∏è $.offers[2].ageRestriction: Recommended property ageRestriction is missing from Offer.
  • ‚ö†Ô∏è $.offers[3].name: Recommended property name is missing from Offer.
  • ‚ö†Ô∏è $.offers[3].ageRestriction: Recommended property ageRestriction is missing from Offer.

‚úÖ Booking should fail if Customer is not included in Order, because we are in AgentBroker mode >> at B or P >> Fetch Opportunities

  • üìù $.eventStatus: Data consumers will assume the eventStatus is scheduled if not specified or invalid.
  • üìù $.superEvent.genderRestriction: Data consumers will assume that there is no gender restriction when no valid genderRestriction is supplied on a SessionSeries.
  • üìù $.superEvent.ageRange: Data consumers will assume that the ageRange is 18+ when not specified.
  • üìù $.superEvent.eventStatus: Data consumers will assume the eventStatus is scheduled if not specified or invalid.
